<div id="review_1608999625" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1608999625" />
    <a title="ambsreads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads"><img alt="ambsreads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1508924675p2/30813900.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1608999625?book_show_action=true">Apr 12, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="ambsreads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="ambsreads" href="/user/show/30813900-ambsreads">ambsreads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17455585-white-hot-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=annoying-male-leads">annoying-male-leads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30813900-ambsreads?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1608999625" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12920137353195469938"><i>White Hot Kiss</i> is the first in its series and a book I've started numerous times and out down. I decided this time I would triumph though and finish it. To my utter surprise I did. I kind of wish I hadn't, it wasn't the greatest book out (but I'll finish the series) and it had a series of issues I found. Most around the characters, both side and main, the dialogue, the love triangle, and the under developed world. <br/><br/><u>Characters</u><br/><br/><b>Layla</b> was our sweet and innocent character. Almost every action of every</span>
  <span id="freeText12920137353195469938" style="display:none"><i>White Hot Kiss</i> is the first in its series and a book I've started numerous times and out down. I decided this time I would triumph though and finish it. To my utter surprise I did. I kind of wish I hadn't, it wasn't the greatest book out (but I'll finish the series) and it had a series of issues I found. Most around the characters, both side and main, the dialogue, the love triangle, and the under developed world. <br /><br /><u>Characters</u><br /><br /><b>Layla</b> was our sweet and innocent character. Almost every action of every character was done to prove just how innocent and virginal she was, including her best friend. She's constantly blushing, flushing, turning red, whatever. Eventually she got better, but the fact that there was a lot of focus on her virginity grew tiresome. The fact she was unable to kiss anyone as well, apart from Roth, got boring as well. She was a bit of a kickass character in the end, but still. <br /><br /><b>Zayne</b> was the "nice guy". But I hated him. I just didn't like his attitude and his superior attitude for what he was. He made promises, but then proceeded not to uphold them. Zayne was a character I wouldn't classify as nice, he is a character I would like to stab 28 times in the chest actually. He was all around crappy and I won't waste my type taking about the arrogant prick. <br /><br /><b>Roth</b> was the "bad boy". I wouldn't go that far though since he was the only decent character. The only definition that would place him under the definition of a bad boy was that he was demon that was also the Crown Prince of hell. Honestly, he was the only one who told Layla the truth and wasn't constantly lying. If she doesn't end up with him I'll be pissed and punch someone. <br /><br /><u>Plot</u><br /><br />Was subpar, it wasn't anything I hadn't read before. It followed the classic storyline of a JLA book and did get a bit cliche in some parts. Apart from that, I did enjoy the book despite the fact I felt a tad bit of a <i>Sweet Evil</i> trilogy vibe. <br /><br /><u>Writing</u><br /><br />It was classic JLA writing. I loved it and I hated it. The dialogue in some parts was cringe worthy and I couldn't see a 17 year old saying it. However, it flowed and I love just love JLA either way. <br /><br /><u>Overall</u> <br /><br />I would give this book a 3.5 overall. It was good. Kept me interested, but wasn't anything I hadn't seen before.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12920137353195469938" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1128001208" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128001208" />
    <a title="Katerina  Kondrenko" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/36306002-katerina-kondrenko"><img alt="Katerina  Kondrenko" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1590049412p2/36306002.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1128001208?book_show_action=true">Dec 09, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katerina  Kondrenko" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katerina  Kondrenko" href="/user/show/36306002-katerina-kondrenko">Katerina  Kondrenko</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9785170878567" href="/book/show/24544486">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=genre-fantasy">genre-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=ships-mine-is-sailing">ships-mine-is-sailing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=writing-nice-humor">writing-nice-humor</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=pov-1st-person">pov-1st-person</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=read-in-russian">read-in-russian</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=pov-female-only">pov-female-only</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=characters-antiheros">characters-antiheros</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=romance-heavy">romance-heavy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/36306002-katerina-kondrenko?shelf=plot-driven-by-everything">plot-driven-by-everything</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1128001208" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10723072269785430822"><blockquote>
  <b>6 out of 10</b>
</blockquote><br/><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br/><a href='http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2015/07/white-hot-kiss-by-jennifer-l-armentrout.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br/><br/><b>Short-Soundtrack:</b><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=yq9R_-6SLYc' rel='nofollow noopener'>AFI– Kiss and control</a><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LSvOTw8UH6s' rel='nofollow noopener'>Starset– My Demons</a><br/><a href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=pH541v-ouag' rel='nofollow noopener'>Royksopp– Here She Comes Again</a><br/><br/><b>Genre</b>: urban-fantasy, YA<br/><b>Stuff</b>: gargoyles, demons, hybrids<br/><b>Fail</b>: typical Armentrout<br/><b>WOW</b>: Astaroth <br/><b>POV</b>: 1st-person, female<br/><b>Love-Geometry</b>: medium<br/><br/><b>Quote-Core</b>: <blockquote>
  <i>
    “People with the purest souls are capable </i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText10723072269785430822" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>6 out of 10</b>
</blockquote><br /><b>Ревью в моем блоге/This review on my blog<br /><a href="http://living-a-thousand-lives.blogspot.ru/2015/07/white-hot-kiss-by-jennifer-l-armentrout.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Living A Thousand Lives</a></b> <i>(please use Chrome/Yandex browser or Android/IOS to see the page; otherwise, spoiler-tags I use to make my post compact may not work)</i><br /><br /><b>Short-Soundtrack:</b><br /><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=yq9R_-6SLYc" rel="nofollow noopener">AFI– Kiss and control</a><br /><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=LSvOTw8UH6s" rel="nofollow noopener">Starset– My Demons</a><br /><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=pH541v-ouag" rel="nofollow noopener">Royksopp– Here She Comes Again</a><br /><br /><b>Genre</b>: urban-fantasy, YA<br /><b>Stuff</b>: gargoyles, demons, hybrids<br /><b>Fail</b>: typical Armentrout<br /><b>WOW</b>: Astaroth <br /><b>POV</b>: 1st-person, female<br /><b>Love-Geometry</b>: medium<br /><br /><b>Quote-Core</b>: <blockquote>
  <i>
    “People with the purest souls are capable of the greatest evils.”
  </i>
</blockquote><br /><b>I’m late for the party.</b> Seems like all the people have already read this book while I was looking in the other direction and even forgot who’s the author of gargoyle’s (wtf) romance. But a couple of chapters and I’ve got it – Jennifer Armentrout. Here we are, with Deamon renamed as Roth, Katy-hybrid with name Layla, school-blah, and a clan of creatures with a problem with breeding… <br /><br /><b>The concept is not bad.</b> Stone guards showed themselves to people, their goal is to secure the earth from evil and humans from the knowledge about demons. Excuse me? People aware of gargoyles living among them, know they protect them from something, but they have no idea from what exactly? What do they think the guards fight? Financial crisis? High taxes? Kid alcoholism? <br /><br /><b>The plot is quite simple.</b> A girl thinks she's <i>that</i> but it turns out that's she's <i>this</i>, and then everyone get that she's <i>something more</i>. The world is in danger, of course. But it’s not the matter. The matter is, Layla has two boys, both are sexy and handsome, but one of them she can’t kiss or else she’ll take his soul, the other one is perfectly kissable, but he’s a demon. What a choice! As to me, I see no problem at all. Why? I’m going to explain….<br /><br /><b>Zayne.</b> A guard with long hair with color of sand (I don’t know how long it is, but he can scrape it back into a ponytail, I didn't forgive such a thing even to Belikov, so I won't make exceptions for someone named Zayne). Huge and strong boy, who likes to call Layla a bug (how nice of him) and daydream (secretly) about her. They can’t be together – Zayne wants to come to heaven after his death where live A… no, not angels – Alphas! But it’s not the only reason – Layla is a half-demon-half-guard (I can’t not to share with you my association: in Russian Stand Up Show a guy was performing with a keyboard and was talking about sounds, he pressed a button named “sluice” and then a button named “horse” and then he made with them a very funny song named half-horse-half-sluice… you see the pattern, yes?), well, she can’t be his mate, no guard can breed with a half-horse… I mean, half-demon-half-guard. And as you see, I’m not a fan of Zayne. He countless times gave up to his father Layla’s secrets, discussed her weaknesses with Layla’s girl-enemy who is a very good mate for Zayne, so Zayne’s father is trying to bring them closer, and overall he acted like an idiot. <br /><br /><b>Roth. </b>Tall brunet with an amazing body and a snarky sense of humor. Demon. Crown Prince of Hell. *pause for laughing* I adore him. He’s awesome. He’s the one sane person in this story. Staying himself till the end he was growing up and becoming a “real boy” (Hello, Pinocchio!). His skin is decorated with a few tattoos (they are alive!), his tongue has piercing, his eyes are gold, he’s a good singer, drives Porsche and reads Po. Moreover, he’s stalking MC, saving her ass, telling her the truth about her heritage and feeds her with cookies. Em… what’s wrong with you, Layla? With Zayne you ate only sweet dough and drank orange juice. Roth is the best!<br /><br /><b>Layla. </b>Typical Katy with all the consequences those come with it. If you haven’t met Katy yet, I’ll tell you what to expect. MC is naive flower which has a few friends and thinks that she’s not pretty while she’s definitely hot as… as an albino with nice curves. A great potential is contained inside of her and she will show the world her true nature, but first you have to make her angry while beating her love interests, both of them (!) or else magic won’t work. <br /><br /><b>The defect</b>: We gonna die! What can we do?! Kiss! Jennifer loves such twists. I don’t mind them too. But maybe we should go somewhere safe and only then would taking our clothes off? <br /><br /><b>Mythology</b> is a grab bag.<br /><br /><b>The process</b>: tones of misunderstandings plus final action-reunion.<br /><br /><b>The ending.</b> Too fulfilled. You can mistake this book for a standalone if not to know better. A few unspoken things wouldn’t hurt. <br /><br /><b>Overall.</b> The writing style is kinda aphrodisiac (Roth knows how to use his mouth (in Russian “Roth” means “Mouth”, so you see what I’m doing here) and not only mouth). MC isn’t bad, not super smart but not annoying either. Love triangle isn’t that obvious in view of the fact that one of the cathetuses aren’t fit our hypotenuse (I heard this reason would somehow resolved in the sequel). It was a very fast and funny read (just think about a snake Bambi, a kitten Thor or a dragon Tumper, all of these cuties belong to Roth as well as my heart).<br /><br />I will continue this series.<br /><br /><b>PS</b>: Zayne, try to hide, so no one would able to find you. <br /><br /><b>The Dark Elements (Тёмные элементы)</b>:<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128001108" rel="nofollow noopener">Bitter Sweet Love (Горько-сладкая любовь)</a> #0.5/3<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128001208" rel="nofollow noopener">White Hot Kiss (Жаркий поцелуй)</a> #1/3<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128001130" rel="nofollow noopener">Stone Cold Touch (Холодные объятия)</a> #2/3<br />— <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1128001146" rel="nofollow noopener">Every Last Breath (Каждый вдох)</a> #3/3 </span>
  <a data-text-id="10723072269785430822" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_3180234612" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3180234612" />
    <a title="Effy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26874718-effy"><img alt="Effy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1603795864p2/26874718.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3180234612?book_show_action=true">Feb 07, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Effy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Effy" href="/user/show/26874718-effy">Effy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17455585-white-hot-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26874718-effy?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26874718-effy?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26874718-effy?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26874718-effy?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26874718-effy?shelf=forbidden-romance">forbidden-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26874718-effy?shelf=slow-burn-romance">slow-burn-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3180234612" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3633234371747130074">“I lost myself the moment I found you.”<br/>I usually avoid reading love triangle novels as much as possible because I tend to develop feelings for one of the two love interests and get bored. Falling for both male characters was new to me. This book was something else.<br/>The novel is a quintessential urban fantasy, paranormal novel set in a place where the stereotypically portrayed as pure, benevolent Wardens coexist with demons. Laya is in the middle. She is half demon, half gargoyle and can see throu</span>
  <span id="freeText3633234371747130074" style="display:none">“I lost myself the moment I found you.”<br />I usually avoid reading love triangle novels as much as possible because I tend to develop feelings for one of the two love interests and get bored. Falling for both male characters was new to me. This book was something else.<br />The novel is a quintessential urban fantasy, paranormal novel set in a place where the stereotypically portrayed as pure, benevolent Wardens coexist with demons. Laya is in the middle. She is half demon, half gargoyle and can see through and feed on souls. She does not fit in, nor does she feel like she belongs to the Wardens' way of life. The only one around whom she does not feel suppressed is Zayne, a delectable gargoyle on whom she has had a crush for years. Her feelings are not completely unreciprocated. Nevertheless, her potential lethal touch on a Warden makes even kissing a possibility off the table. Her unspeakable desire for Zayne diminishes when she crosses paths with Roth, a smug demon who is conveniently showing up at the most opportune moments to save the damsel in distress. <br />I have to admit that the novel lacks plausibility as regards the plot since the world seems to center around Layla and her indecision to choose a guy. She annoyingly keeps flirting with both Roth and Zayne and experiences different feelings for each one respectively. <br />I am in the minority who rooted for Zayne and Layla although I can see why many readers go for Roth. Zayne's character was fleshed out and I wholeheartedly felt for him. He was mysterious, caring and protective. What's not to love about him? Roth was the typical enigmatic, pompous guy who would normally make my heart pound in my chest. This time Zayne won me over and increased my heart palpitations.<br />This audiobook kept me on the edge of my seat and I cannot wait to continue reading the series.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3633234371747130074" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1158040186" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1158040186" />
    <a title="bibliophile (Romance Addict) " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict"><img alt="bibliophile (Romance Addict) " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1427910066p2/17937691.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1158040186?book_show_action=true">Jan 06, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="bibliophile (Romance Addict) " class="user" itemprop="url" name="bibliophile (Romance Addict) " href="/user/show/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict">bibliophile (Romance Addict) </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17455585-white-hot-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=love-triangle">love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=enemies-to-lovers">enemies-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=ya">ya</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17937691-bibliophile-romance-addict?shelf=kick-ass-heroine">kick-ass-heroine</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1158040186" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4053841348519284108"><br/><br/><b>Five *demons* stars!!</b><br/><br/>This is book one of the The Dark Elements trilogy by Jennifer Armentrout, and oh my God! Jen never failed me, or dissappointed me. I love this book, and every charater, and just EVERYTHING!! <br/><br/>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨<br/> <br/>The story: In this book, we follow a girl called Layla. She's half Warren, half demon, and she hates this fact so much. She lives with her fellow Warrens, and her life is fine until she meets Roth. <br/> <br/>Roth is badass, hottie, and a demon! Layla hates his guts, but she can't handle </span>
  <span id="freeText4053841348519284108" style="display:none"><br><br><b>Five *demons* stars!!</b><br><br>This is book one of the The Dark Elements trilogy by Jennifer Armentrout, and oh my God! Jen never failed me, or dissappointed me. I love this book, and every charater, and just EVERYTHING!! <br><br>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨<br> <br>The story: In this book, we follow a girl called Layla. She's half Warren, half demon, and she hates this fact so much. She lives with her fellow Warrens, and her life is fine until she meets Roth. <br> <br>Roth is badass, hottie, and a demon! Layla hates his guts, but she can't handle him. (I don't blame her since he's HOT!) That's not the only problem for Layla since being with Roth is like stabbing her family and Zayne in the back. <br><br>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨<br><br><a href="http://s1219.photobucket.com/user/meemoo229/media/IMG_0408.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431889902i/14878939._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo IMG_0408.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br> <br>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“You need something," he said, and when I stared at him, he added, "Your face."<br>"My face?"<br>"It's in need of my kisses.” </blockquote>
</b><br><br>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨<br><br><b>Characters:<br> <br>Layla:</b><br> <br>Layla is a half demon, half Warren. She has no idea who are her parents, and so she lives with the Warrens. Layla's life is 'perfect' because she goes to school, and lives her life almost regularly. However, when she meets Roth, he makes her realize that she was fooled all along. The love she had for Zayne decreases as Roth makes her experience so many new things she could have never done before. <br> <br>What made me like Layla is the fact that she didn't histate to hide some secrets from her 'family'. Even though she knew they were hiding so many facts from her, she just never felt sorry. She grows stronger throughout the book which is also great. <br> <br><b>Roth:</b><br> <br>Roth is just amazing. I like his personality. His comebacks. I like how he treats Layla, and how sweet he is. I also like Bambi, and the fact that it always help Layla. Roth is perfect in every way, and I have to admit I'm so team Roth! Give me a YA book that I didn't choose a team?<br> <br> <br> <br>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨ <br><br><b>Positives:</b> <br> <br>1) Roth! This comes as no surprise since Roth became one of my book boyfriends from the start of the book. He's just great with amazing comebacks. I love the way he teases Layla, and I honestly feel like layla doesn't deserve him. I love how he's a demon and still kind and caring. <br><br>2) Layla: Okay, so I don't like many heroines, but Layla is kinda awesome. She's not weak, and has her own thinking. Although she made me pissed at some parts *cough* *cough* (Roth is wrapped around her finger!) *cough*<br> <br>3) Plot: I really like the plot because so many plot twists happened. I love the fact that Roth and Layla started off as enemies, and ended up pretty close (Pretty cliche but who cares?) <br> <br>4) The character development. When I started reading this book, Layla was protected by everyone around her. She wasn't cared much for, and is always on the side. By the end of the book, she's a strong character who knows how to protect herslef. She can see whose on her side, and whose not. <br> <br>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨<br> <br><b>
  <blockquote>“At some point, Roth had gotten hold of my cell and replaced Zayne's name with Stony and listed his own number under Sexy Beast. What a tool” <br> <br>-❤<br> <br>“Then I guess I'll just have to try biting again"<br>"You wanna try?" He leaned the curve of my cheek. "Let me suggest more appropriate places. I have this piercing.” </blockquote>
</b><br> <br> <br>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨<br> <br><b>Negative:</b><br> <br>1) Zayne: In this book, I don't think there are two teams. There is only TeamRoth because Zayne doesn't even have a chance! He was completely engrossed with his own stupid ideas when so many things were happening around him. He is so ignorant, and always pity himself, and I just Dislike him!!! <br><br>2) All the Warren community! Ugh!! I mean they act like they're perfect, and pure, while they suck, and needs to learn respect. I just think that Layla is a bit stupid because she stick with them. SMH!!<br> <br>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨<br> <br><b>Favorite part: </b> when Roth saves Layla for the hundredth time, and take her to his apartment!! God!! That was the best sleepover I read in a book. ☻<br> <br>Ending: The ending was OMG!!! I wanted more from Roth, but it's fine. There are two more books in the series so I will forgive Jennifer for the ending this time. <br> <br>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨<br> <br><b>
  <blockquote>“If i say thank you, will you go away?"<br>"Yes"<br>"Thank you" I said eagerly.<br>"I lied"<br>"What?" I looked up at him, frowning. "That's messed up” </blockquote>
</b><br> <br> <br>▨▨▨▨▨▨▨▨<br><br>I rated this five stars because it was a very good book. I would defintely complete reading the series, but I'm still waiting for the third book to come out. I seriously can't wait. So, this book is also added to many favroite books list. It was an entertaining, action packed book. <br> <br><b>Heroine: 4 stars.<br>Hero: 5 stars (DUHHHH!!)<br>Romance level: 5 stars.<br>Ending: 4 stars.<br>Plot: 5 stars.<br>Writing style: 5 stars (I love Jennifer Almentrout's writing.) <br><br>Recommendation:</b> I recommend this to every Fantasy/Romance readers out there. This has a very unique storyline, and will definitely an interesting read. </span>
  <a data-text-id="4053841348519284108" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer7681398309234887012"><b>

  <span id="freeText7681398309234887012" style="display:none"><b>
  <a href="http://www.amazon.com/White-Hot-Kiss-Dark-Elements/dp/0373211104/ref=as_sl_pc_ss_til?tag=fandmontmaga-20&amp;linkCode=w01&amp;linkId=2JZHUV4ZDIYXBBWQ&amp;creativeASIN=0373211104" rel="nofollow noopener">Buy this book on AMAZON</a>

</b><br /><br /><b>4 of 5 stars (Please read my rating system further below).</b> I would've rated this book more like a 3.8-3.9 but I upped my rating because why not. I loved the characters in this book and they're chemistry with each other, it was fascinating! The foreshadowing was all over the place and kept me on the edge of my seat at all times and it was exhilarating. The world building was a little bit rough in the beginning, but as the story developed it solidified and made the story so much more real, I loved it! I would definitely recommend this book to anyone who loves adventure, supernatural powers, and one heck of a good love triangle. <br /><br /><b>My rating system</b>: (I <b>do</b> use half stars.)<br /><b>5</b> - <b>I do not use the 5 star</b>. Not because a book might not be worthy, but because a book is never perfect.<br /><b>4</b> - I <b>loved</b> it! There weren't too many flaws, and I had no trouble getting through it. (A 4 star rating is the highest rating I've ever given a book.)<br /><b>3</b> - I <b>enjoyed</b> the book, but there we're flaws that made me enjoy it less.<br /><b>2</b> - I <b>finished</b> the book, but there were too many flaws for me to enjoy it.<br /><b>1</b> - I <b>could not finish</b> the book, and I probably did not finish it....</span>

<div id="review_1146120246" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1146120246" />
    <a title="Cody" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35007929-cody"><img alt="Cody" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1415626292p2/35007929.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1146120246?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Cody" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Cody" href="/user/show/35007929-cody">Cody</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17455585-white-hot-kiss">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1146120246" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6261238743037114868"><b>I COULD READ THIS A THOUSAND TIMES AND STILL LOVE IT!</b><br/><br/>This was my first book by Jennifer L. Armentrout and I think it will forever be a favourite of mine. Don’t get me wrong every book or series she releases I become obsessed with to the point were they get 5 stars because I haven’t moved off my ass for hours because I can’t bear to part from the book and compare every other book boyfriend on the planet to her gorgeous characters… <i>This isn’t sad at all!</i><br/><br/>So when it came to reading White Hot Kiss ag</span>
  <span id="freeText6261238743037114868" style="display:none"><b>I COULD READ THIS A THOUSAND TIMES AND STILL LOVE IT!</b><br /><br />This was my first book by Jennifer L. Armentrout and I think it will forever be a favourite of mine. Don’t get me wrong every book or series she releases I become obsessed with to the point were they get 5 stars because I haven’t moved off my ass for hours because I can’t bear to part from the book and compare every other book boyfriend on the planet to her gorgeous characters… <i>This isn’t sad at all!</i><br /><br />So when it came to reading White Hot Kiss again, I was absolutely thrilled to find it was like reading the book a fresh with all the plot twists, drama, tension, angst and FEELS!<br /><br />JLA manages to make people made of stone sexy and demons with some interesting piercings and tattoo’s the hottest people on the planet. When she decides to write a male love interest she <i>does not</i> hold back.<br /><br />Naturally we have two warring enemies The Wardens (gargoyles) and The Demons. Layla is a hybrid of the two; because of this she can see people’s souls and leave a ‘mark’ on a Demon that only The Warden’s can see and use to hunt them. Warden Zayne is Layla's best friend and childhood crush but he still treats her as an annoying friend/sister, nothing can ever happen between them; Layla can’t kiss anyone with a soul and Zayne has the purest soul, to do so would kill him. <i>Perfect!</i><br /><br />Enter Roth, the baddest thing in town; Roth, a demon who also happens to be the most alluring, sexy, arrogant person ever… and that whole nothing kissing people with a soul? Not a problem here, demons don’t have souls. Layla is helpless to Roth’s antic’s, she knows he’s bad news, if the Wardens found her even speaking to a demon she would be branded a traitor but what can she do when he turns up at her school, the park and even the bathroom? There's only so much resisting a girl can do!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“At some point, Roth had gotten hold of my cell and replaced Zayne's name with Stony and listed his own number under Sexy Beast. What a tool. I grinned.”</i>
</b><br /><br />I’m sure it’s obvious that this book will feature a love triangle but trust me you will not mind it but if you really do oppose them I would still give this book a try as it’s much more focused on one side of the triangle and not a pissing contest at every turn. The romance is sizzling as JLA always pushes the boundaries on YA, which I love! It does get a little cheesy at times and maybe you want more action but it really doesn't take anything away from the story and truly these thoughts only enter your mind after you've read the book and reflect on it.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I think you like me," Roth said suddenly.<br />I stopped pacing and my heart did a funny little jump. "What? No."<br />He tilted his head to the side, his lips spreading into a teasing grin. "The way you lie to yourself is sort of cute."<br />"I'm not lying."<br />"Hmm..." He sat up, eyes glimmering with mirth. "You wanted me to kiss you earlier.”<br />Heat flooded my cheeks. "No. I did not."<br />"You're right. You wanted me to do much, much more."</i>
</b><br /><br />This was such a <b>fun</b> read, even the secondary characters were amazing, this book is filled with sexual tension, forbidden romance, childhood-crushes and a lot of humour that will have you laughing along the way. The cliffhanger for me was heartbreaking, it was no less traumatic reading it the second time around.. some series sacrifices are made!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“I lost myself the moment I found you.”</i>
</b><br /><br /><a href="http://literary-lyobsessed.blogspot.co.uk" rel="nofollow noopener">Literary-ly Obsessed</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6261238743037114868" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer784874448" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9969254959977795773"><a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com'>www.melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com</a><br/><br/>I thought this book was awesome! I loved the characters. Layla is so cool and she used a lot of phrases that I use in the real world. :) She did a few stupid things in the book and only one led to some distressing moments, but I felt after it was done, it was all for the better. It's so hard to talk about this without spoilers! <br/><br/>So Layla is half demon and half warden (gargoyle) but she doesn't have any powers or does she? She lives with the Wardens that keep de</span>
  <span id="freeText9969254959977795773" style="display:none"><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com">www.melissa413readsalot.blogspot.com</a><br><br>I thought this book was awesome! I loved the characters. Layla is so cool and she used a lot of phrases that I use in the real world. :) She did a few stupid things in the book and only one led to some distressing moments, but I felt after it was done, it was all for the better. It's so hard to talk about this without spoilers! <br><br>So Layla is half demon and half warden (gargoyle) but she doesn't have any powers or does she? She lives with the Wardens that keep demons in line, but she can't change and fly like they can, the only thing she can do is a tag on a demon for the wardens to hunt. She feels pretty useless. <br><br>She goes to a regular school and has a couple of friends, they don't know what she is though. She usually goes out for a bit after school to tag demons and then one of the peeps from home picks her up at a certain time. <br><br>She has a best friend named Zayne that she grew up with, she secretly loves him, but can never be with him because she's not a pure blood. Well, I think that sucks for her. <br><br>Then she meets a demon named Roth who saves her life several times. He's actually a good demon, sounds weird huh? And... he is the only one that tells her who her mom really is and why all of the sudden all of these demons are coming after her. He holds nothing back from her, where her family at the house haven't told her anything. And it is freaking wicked when you find out the story of her life and her mom especially! <br><br>This book is just so good. I am so glad I found it from some GR friends on here and can read the trilogy! Unless it's going to be an ongoing series then that would be awesome too! I already have the next two books and I hope to get to them soon because that ENDING! <br><br>I did love the part where Layla lets go when her...hmmm..I guess you could say.. loves (Zayne &amp; Roth) are in harms way. She freaking.. oh I can't tell you. Let's just say she's a force to be reckoned with and then some. <br><br><a href="http://s1379.photobucket.com/user/melmartD11/media/book%20banner_zpsh916lrql.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('zwYTxA2ExeWwaTiMbuM8JfRGNqhTIeMCaptv5lKJFGUkZwvoeRLrY2ny2pGtIevoe4ZFucWHwHEet2XWCPAQWQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('q5JeTReKGEnAxjwo+QMtbQGYXuZudqM0+5VPIUgiEtpA80ZhYxw2zxld3jU6wfqgjlgt9/jQgEePuUURElsW5g==')})
  }
//]]>

All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText6291396679861603453" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>

</div>
